#!/bin/sh

PATH=/spec/opt/SUNWspro/bin/:/usr/bin:/usr/ccs/bin:/usr/sbin:/sbin
export PATH

# Informationals
echo My system name is `hostname`
STARTDIR=`pwd`
cd tools/src
echo The current directory is `pwd`
echo My username is `/usr/ucb/whoami`
echo 'uname output (but you knew that by looking):'
uname -a
echo "path is '$PATH'"
echo Compiler version:
cc -V 

# Settings necessary for build
ulimit -s 128000
BZIP2CFLAGS="-fast -xtarget=generic"
export BZIP2CFLAGS
MD5CFLAGS="-fast -xtarget=generic"
export MD5CFLAGS
PERLFLAGS="-Doptimize=-fast -Aoptimize=-xtarget=generic -Aoptimize=-xO4 -Dcc=cc"
export PERLFLAGS

# The build itself
echo
echo
sleep 3
time ./buildtools 
echo
echo

# Some (limited) proof of the build
cd $STARTDIR
pwd
. ./shrc
runspec -V
specperl -V
